		<script>
			/**
			 * When the main stylesheet loads, remove the hide-fouc class from the body
			 */
			var styles = document.getElementById( 'chive-theme-css-css' ) || document.querySelector( 'link[id^="all-css"]' );
			var removeFoucStyles = function() {
				document.querySelector( 'html' ).classList.remove( 'hide-fouc' );
			}

			if ( styles ) {
				if ( styles.sheet ) {
					removeFoucStyles();
				} else {
					styles.addEventListener( 'load', function() {
						removeFoucStyles();
					} );
				}
			}

			// Fallback for if for some reason JS doesn't detect the stylesheet loading
			setTimeout( function() {
				removeFoucStyles();
			}, 3000 );
		</script>
